            <script>
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", (event) => {
            // gsap code here!
            const carouselInner = document.querySelector('.carousel_inner');

            // Function to animate
            function animateCarousel() {
                // Calculate the width of a single item
                const itemWidth = carouselInner.querySelector('.logo_clients').offsetWidth;

                // GSAP animation to slide to the left
                const tl = gsap.timeline({
                    repeat: -1, // Infinite loop
                    defaults: {
                        ease: "none"
                    }
                });

                // Move the first item to the end and reset position seamlessly
                tl.to(carouselInner, {
                    x: -itemWidth,
                    duration: 4,
                    modifiers: {
                        x: gsap.utils.unitize(x => parseFloat(x) % (itemWidth * carouselInner.children
                            .length))
                    },
                    onComplete: () => {
                        carouselInner.appendChild(carouselInner.firstElementChild);
                        gsap.set(carouselInner, {
                            x: 50
                        });
                    }
                });
            }

            animateCarousel();
        });
    </script>
    <script>
        const errorRequired = "This field is required";

    <script src="/assets/scripts/form-quote.js?id=9fab13f98658061036f3aa02322204cd"></script>
    <script>
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
            const formsInput = document.querySelectorAll(".form-inputs input, .form-inputs select");
            const submitButton = document.getElementById("button-get-quote");

            formsInput.forEach(function(input) {
                input.addEventListener("input", checkInputs);
            });

            function isValidEmail(email) {
                const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
                return emailRegex.test(email);
            }

            function isValidURL(url) {
                const urlRegex = /^(www\.)?[a-zA-Z0-9-]+\.[a-zA-Z]{2,}(\.[a-zA-Z]{2,})?$/;
                return urlRegex.test(url);
            }

            function checkInputs() {
                let empty = false;
                formsInput.forEach(function(input) {

                    if (input.value === '') {
                        empty = true;
                    }
                });

                if (empty) {
                    submitButton.disabled = true;
                } else {
                    submitButton.disabled = false;
                }
            }
        });
    </script>
    <script>
        $('#selectPosition').select2({
            allowClear: true,
            placeholder: 'Pilih posisi',
            tags: true,
            theme: 'bootstrap-5',
            createTag: function(params) {
                var dataService = $.trim(params.term);

                if (dataService === '') {
                    return null;
                }

                return {
                    id: dataService,
                    text: dataService,
                    newOption: true
                };
            },
        })
    </script>
    <script>
        const displayMinutes = document.getElementById('minutes');
        const displaySeconds = document.getElementById('seconds');
        const seperate = document.getElementById('seperate');
        const daftarBtn = document.getElementById('daftar');
        const statusInput = document.getElementById('status-regist');
        const desc = document.getElementById('desc-timer');

        function startTimer(duration, displayMinutes, displaySeconds, seperate, daftarBtn) {
            let timer = duration,
                minutes, seconds;
            const interval = setInterval(function() {
                minutes = parseInt(timer / 60, 10);
                seconds = parseInt(timer % 60, 10);

                minutes = minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes;
                seconds = seconds < 10 ? "0" + seconds : seconds;

                displayMinutes.textContent = minutes;
                displaySeconds.textContent = seconds;
                daftarBtn.textContent = "Register Now!";
                desc.innerHTML = "Get Consultation Quota Now!";
                statusInput.value = '1';
                displayMinutes.classList.add('border','background-danger-70', 'text-white');
                displaySeconds.classList.add('border', 'background-danger-70' ,'text-white');
                daftarBtn.classList.remove('background-transparent', 'text-purple-30', 'border-purple-30');
                daftarBtn.classList.add('background-purple-70', 'text-white', 'border-purple-70');

                if (--timer < 0) {
                    displayMinutes.textContent = "00";
                    displaySeconds.textContent = "00";
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    daftarBtn.textContent = "Regist as Waiting List!";
                    desc.innerHTML = "Oops, you are late to register. But don't worry, you can still get on the Waiting List."
                    statusInput.value = '0';
                    displayMinutes.classList.remove('border-danger-70', 'background-danger-70' ,'text-white');
                    displaySeconds.classList.remove('border-danger-70', 'background-danger-70' ,'text-white');
                    daftarBtn.classList.remove('background-purple-70', 'text-white', 'border-purple-70');
                    daftarBtn.classList.add('background-transparent', 'text-purple-30', 'border-purple-30');
                }
            }, 1000);
        }

        function initTimer() {
            let now = new Date();
            const storedTime = localStorage.getItem('timer-amber');

            if (storedTime) {
                const startTime = new Date(storedTime);
                const elapsedTime = Math.floor((now - startTime) / 1000); // time in seconds

                if (elapsedTime > 600) {
                    daftarBtn.textContent = "Regist as Waiting List!";
                    desc.innerHTML = "Oops, you are late to register. But don't worry, you can still get on the Waiting List.";
                    statusInput.value = '0';
                    displayMinutes.classList.remove('border-danger-70', 'background-danger-70' ,'text-white');
                    displaySeconds.classList.remove('border-danger-70', 'background-danger-70' ,'text-white');
                    daftarBtn.classList.remove('background-purple-70', 'text-white', 'border-purple-70');
                    daftarBtn.classList.add('background-transparent', 'text-purple-30', 'border-purple-30');
                } else {
                    startTimer(600 - elapsedTime, displayMinutes, displaySeconds, seperate, daftarBtn);
                }
            } else {
                localStorage.setItem('timer-amber', now);
                startTimer(600, displayMinutes, displaySeconds, seperate, daftarBtn);
            }
        }

        initTimer();
    </script>

    <script>
    function initializeCarousel(carouselId, duration = 50) {
        const carousel = document.getElementById(carouselId);
        if (carousel) {
            const carouselIndicators = carousel.querySelectorAll(".carousel-indicators button span");
            let intervalID;

            const reviewCarousel = new bootstrap.Carousel(carousel);

            window.addEventListener("load", function() {
                fillCarouselIndicator(1);
            });

            carousel.addEventListener("slide.bs.carousel", function(e) {
                let index = e.to;
                fillCarouselIndicator(++index);
            });

            function fillCarouselIndicator(index) {
                let i = 0;
                for (const carouselIndicator of carouselIndicators) {
                    if (carouselIndicator)
                        carouselIndicator.style.width = 0;
                }
                clearInterval(intervalID);
                reviewCarousel.pause();

                intervalID = setInterval(function() {
                    i++;

                    const spanLoader = carousel.querySelector(".carousel-indicators .active span")
                    if (spanLoader)
                        spanLoader.style.width = i + "%";


                    if (i >= 100)
                        reviewCarousel.next();

                }, duration);
            }
        }
    }
</script>

        function displayText() {

        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
            let menuSection = document.querySelectorAll('.cover-tab');
            let link = document.querySelectorAll('.cover-tab-link');

            // for clickable event
            menuSection.forEach(v => {
                v.onclick = (() => {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        menuSection.forEach(j => j.classList.remove('active'))
                        v.classList.add('active')
                    }, 300)
                })
            })

            link.forEach(v => {
                v.onclick = (() => {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        link.forEach(j => j.classList.remove('active'))
                        v.classList.add('active')
                    }, 300)
                })
            })

            // for window scrolldown event
            window.onscroll = function() {
                let mainSection = document.querySelectorAll('main section');
                let link = document.querySelectorAll('.cover-tab-link');
                let active = document.querySelector('.cover-tab-link.active');
                let container = document.querySelector('.cover-tab-container');
                let tabContainer = document.querySelector('#tabContainer');
                let scrollOffset = active.offsetLeft - 32;

                mainSection.forEach((v, i) => {
                    let rect = v.getBoundingClientRect().y
                    if (rect < window.innerHeight - 500) {
                        menuSection.forEach(v => v.classList.remove('active'))

                    }
                })
            }
